       <script>
        window.addEventListener('message', function(e) {
 				var obj_iframe = jQuery(".ad_pushdown iframe");
 				var eventName = e.data[0];
 				var data = e.data[1];
 
 				switch( eventName ) {
 					// Resize the IFRAME to whatever size the IFRAME's contents want.
 					case 'pushdownSetHeight': 
 						obj_iframe.parent().height(data);
 				  		obj_iframe.height(data);
 				  		break;
 				  	// Once the IFRAME's contents have loaded, decide what size image to load.
 				  	case 'pushdownLoaded': 
 				  		obj_iframe.width('100%');
 				  		obj_iframe.css('max-width', '100%');
 
 				  		var iframe = document.getElementsByClassName('ad_pushdown_wrapper')[0].getElementsByTagName('iframe')[0];
 
 				  		// If no "ad_pushdown_stay_minimized" yet exists, send a message to show the expanded size ad, and set 
 				  		// the cookie for the session so you only see the expanded ad once.
 				  		// Else send a message to show the minimized ad.
 				  		if ( document.cookie.match(/^(.*;)?\s*ad_pushdown_stay_minimized\s*=\s*[^;]+(.*)?$/) == null ) {
 				    		iframe.contentWindow.postMessage(["showExpanded", '1'], "*"); 
 
 				    		var now = new Date();
 							var time = now.getTime();
 							time += 43200 * 1000;
 							now.setTime(time);
 
 				    		document.cookie = "ad_pushdown_stay_minimized=1; expires=" + now.toUTCString() + "; path=/";
 				    	}
 				    	else {
 				    		iframe.contentWindow.postMessage(["showMinimized", '1'], "*"); 
 				    	}
 				  		break;
 			  	}
 			}, false);
 
 	    	window.CFLAdUtility.displayAd('CFL_Network_Pushdown', 'ad_pushdown_1', [[1270, 90]]);
       </script>

        <div id="ad_bigbox_2" style="margin: auto auto; width: 300px; height: 250px;">
         <script>
          function display_ad_bigbox_2_8111() {
 	    		var int_width = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth;
 		    	var display_ad = false;
 
 		    	var use_breakpoint_restriction = '1';
 		    	var sm = 768;
 				var md = 1024;
 				var lg = 1250;
 		        if ( use_breakpoint_restriction == '1' ) {
 		        	if ( 'lg' == 'lg' && (int_width >= lg) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + lg);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'lg' == 'xs' && (int_width < sm) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' < ' + sm);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'lg' == 'sm,md' && (int_width >= sm && int_width < lg) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + sm + ' && ' + int_width + ' < ' + lg);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'lg' == 'xs,lg' && (int_width < sm || int_width >= lg) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'lg' == 'sm,md,lg' && (int_width >= sm) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        }
 		        else {
 		        	display_ad = true;
 		        }
 		        
 		        if ( display_ad === true ) {
 		        	window.CFLAdUtility.displayAd('CFL_Network_BigBox', 'ad_bigbox_2', [300, 250]);        	
 	    	
 	    			//console.log('Displaying big box 2');
 		        }
 	    	}
 	    	display_ad_bigbox_2_8111();
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>

           function display_ad_bigbox_5_1754() {
 	    		var int_width = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth;
 		    	var display_ad = false;
 
 		    	var use_breakpoint_restriction = '1';
 		    	var sm = 768;
 				var md = 1024;
 				var lg = 1250;
 		        if ( use_breakpoint_restriction == '1' ) {
 		        	if ( 'xs' == 'lg' && (int_width >= lg) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + lg);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'xs' == 'xs' && (int_width < sm) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' < ' + sm);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'xs' == 'sm,md' && (int_width >= sm && int_width < lg) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + sm + ' && ' + int_width + ' < ' + lg);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'xs' == 'xs,lg' && (int_width < sm || int_width >= lg) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'xs' == 'sm,md,lg' && (int_width >= sm) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        }
 		        else {
 		        	display_ad = true;
 		        }
 		        
 		        if ( display_ad === true ) {
 		        	window.CFLAdUtility.displayAd('CFL_Network_BigBox', 'ad_bigbox_5', [300, 250]);        	
 	    	
 	    			//console.log('Displaying big box 5');
 		        }
 	    	}
 	    	display_ad_bigbox_5_1754();
          </script>

 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'xs,lg' == 'xs' && (int_width < sm) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' < ' + sm);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'xs,lg' == 'sm,md' && (int_width >= sm && int_width < lg) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + sm + ' && ' + int_width + ' < ' + lg);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'xs,lg' == 'xs,lg' && (int_width < sm || int_width >= lg) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'xs,lg' == 'sm,md,lg' && (int_width >= sm) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        }
 		        else {
 		        	display_ad = true;
 		        }
 		        
 		        if ( display_ad === true ) {
 		        	window.CFLAdUtility.displayAd('CFL_Network_BigBox', 'ad_bigbox_6', [300, 250]);        	
 	    	
 	    			//console.log('Displaying big box 6');
 		        }
 	    	}
 	    	display_ad_bigbox_6_8539();
          </script>
         </div>
        </div>

         <script>
          function display_ad_bigbox_3_2088() {
 	    		var int_width = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth;
 		    	var display_ad = false;
 
 		    	var use_breakpoint_restriction = '1';
 		    	var sm = 768;
 				var md = 1024;
 				var lg = 1250;
 		        if ( use_breakpoint_restriction == '1' ) {
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'lg' && (int_width >= lg) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + lg);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'xs' && (int_width < sm) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' < ' + sm);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'sm,md' && (int_width >= sm && int_width < lg) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + sm + ' && ' + int_width + ' < ' + lg);
 
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'xs,lg' && (int_width < sm || int_width >= lg) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'sm,md,lg' && (int_width >= sm) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        }
 		        else {
 		        	display_ad = true;
 		        }
 		        
 		        if ( display_ad === true ) {
 		        	window.CFLAdUtility.displayAd('CFL_Network_BigBox', 'ad_bigbox_3', [300, 250]);        	
 	    	
 	    			//console.log('Displaying big box 3');
 		        }
 	    	}
 	    	display_ad_bigbox_3_2088();
         </script>

 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + lg);

 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'xs' && (int_width < sm) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' < ' + sm);

 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'sm,md' && (int_width >= sm && int_width < lg) ) {
 		        		//console.log(int_width + ' >= ' + sm + ' && ' + int_width + ' < ' + lg);

 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'xs,lg' && (int_width < sm || int_width >= lg) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        	if ( 'sm,md' == 'sm,md,lg' && (int_width >= sm) ) {
 		        		display_ad = true;
 		        	}
 		        }
 		        else {
 		        	display_ad = true;
 		        }
